 Those who heard the lion at the 17th annual jashn-e-bahar Mushaira in Delhi on Friday did not believe their eyes once because the person who heard the lion was not an Indian or Pakistani, but the 75-year-old poet Zhang Shiguan of China
 jhang ne apana 'pan nem' intikhaab alam rakhaa he, jo unke chini naam kaa urdu anuwaad he
 Mughal-era Ramlila written in Urdu became a miljunoon, not a Urdu language, a passion for Urdu Chinese poet Zhang
 unhone bataaya, '1963 kii baat he
 i was in the final year of graduation
 tab mujhe apni sarkaar kii taraf se urdu padhane ke liye kaha gaya kyonki china bharat or pakistan ke saath kareebi sambandh bananaa chahta tha
 i initially felt bad because my passion was journalism, but i fell in love with it when i started reading this language
 'urdu ne karai shadijhang ne bataaya ki unhone chaar saal tak saat student ke group saath urdu padhi
 There was also a girl in the same group, whom Zhang later married
 is group ne urdu kii padhai beijing broadcasting institute main kii thi, jise ab communication uniwarsity of china ke naam se pahachaanaa jaataa he
 Zhang later became the editor of the Urdu edition of a monthly magazine called China Pictorial
 salanaa jashn-e-bahaar mushaayare main chaar baar shirkat kar chuke jhang ne kaha, 'jab bhashaa par meri puri pakad ban gai, to maine urdu main sher likhane shuru kar die

 - Input IANS akshay tritiya ke maukey par somvaar ko gangotri, yamunotri or kedarnath ke kapaat shraddhaluon ke liye khol die jaaenge
 With this, the famous annual Chardham Yatra of the Garhwal Himalaya will begin
 aadhikarik sutron ne ravivaar ko bataaya ki uttarkashi jile main das hajaar feet se zyada kii oonchai par sthit gangotri or yamunotri mandir tathaa rudraprayag jile main 11 hajaar feet kii oonchai par sthit kedarnath mandir ke kapaat khulne ke sambandh main sabhi taiyaariyaan puri kar lee gai he
 The doors of these dhams will be opened for devotees after being closed for six months in winter
 gadhwal himalay ke chaar dhaamon ke naam se prasiddh ek anya dham chamoli jile me sthit badrinaath mandir ke kapaat bhi 11 may ko shraddhaluon ke liye khulenge
 The shrines of these dhams are closed every year in the winter due to heavy snowfall of the region for darshan of devotees, which are reopened when summer comes
 tippaniyan During the six-month travel season, lakhs of devotees come from all over the country and abroad to visit these shrines
 chardhaam yatra ko gadhwal himalay kii aarthiki kii ridh bhi mana jaataa he
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
